event.\n41\ttype Event struct {\n42\t\tID         int64     `json:\"id\"`\n43\t\tTimestamp  int64     `json:\"timestamp_ms\"`\n44\t\tType       string    `json:\"type\"`\n45\t\tZone       string    `json:\"zone,omitempty\"`\n46\t\tPerson     string    `json:\"person,omitempty\"`\n47\t\tBlobID     int       `json:\"blob_id,omitempty\"`\n48\t\tDetailJSON string    `json:\"detail_json,omitempty\"`\n49\t\tSeverity   string    `json:\"severity\"`\n50\t}\n51\t\n52\t// LogEvent logs a new event to the database and broadcasts it.\n53\tfunc (h *EventsHandler) LogEvent(eventType string, timestamp time.Time, zone, person string, blobID int, detailJSON string, severity string) error {\n54\t\th.mu.Lock()\n55\t\tdefer h.mu.Unlock()\n56\t\n57\t\tts := timestamp.UnixNano() / 1e6\n58\t\tif severity == \"\" {\n59\t\t\tseverity = \"info\"\n60\t\t}\n61\t\n62\t\tresult, err := h.db.Exec(`\n63\t\t\tINSERT INTO events (timestamp_ms, type, zone, person, blob_id, detail_json, severity)\n64\t\t\tVALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n65\t\t`, ts, eventType, zone, person, blobID, detailJSON, severity)\n66\t\tif err != nil {\n67\t\t\treturn err\n68\t\t}\n69\t\n70\t\tid, _ := result.LastInsertId()\n71\t\n72\t\t// Broadcast to dashboard clients\n73\t\tif h.hub != nil {\n74\t\t\th.hub.BroadcastEventFromDB(id, ts, eventType, zone, person, blobID, detailJSON, severity)\n75\t\t}\n76\t\n77\t\treturn nil\n78\t}\n79\t\n80\t// SetHub sets the dashboard hub for broadcasting events.\n81\tfunc (e *EventsHandler) SetHub(hub DashboardHub) {\n82\t\te.mu.Lock()\n83\t\tdefer e.mu.Unlock()\n84\t\te.hub = hub\n85\t}\n86\t\n87\t// SetFeedbackHandler sets the feedback handler for event feedback endpoints.\n88\tfunc (e *EventsHandler) SetFeedbackHandler(handler any) {\n89\t\te.mu.Lock()\n90\t\tdefer e.mu.Unlock()\n91\t\te.feedbackHandler = handler\n92\t}\n93\t\n94\t// NewEventsHandler creates a new events handler backed by a SQLite file at dbPath.\n95\t// It opens the database, creates the schema, and takes ownership of the connection.\n96\t// Use Close() to release resources.\n97\tfunc NewEventsHandler(dbPath string) (*EventsHandler, error) {\n98\t\tdb, err := sql.Open(\"sqlite\", dbPath)\n99\t\tif err != nil {\n100\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open events db: %w\", err)\n101\t\t}\n102\t\tif err := createEventsSchema(db); err != nil {\n103\t\t\tdb.Close()\n104\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"init events schema: %w\", err)\n105\t\t}\n106\t\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] Events handler initialized (own DB: %s)\", dbPath)\n107\t\treturn &EventsHandler{db: db, ownsDB: true}, nil\n108\t}\n109\t\n110\t// NewEventsHandlerFromDB creates a new events handler using an existing database connection.\n111\t// The events table schema must already exist (created by migrations 001 and 011).\n112\tfunc NewEventsHandlerFromDB(db *sql.DB) *EventsHandler {\n113\t\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] Events handler initialized (shared DB)\")\n114\t\treturn &EventsHandler{db: db}\n115\t}\n116\t\n117\t// Close releases resources. If the handler owns the DB connection, it closes it.\n118\tfunc (e *EventsHandler) Close() {\n119\t\tif e.ownsDB {\n120\t\t\te.db.Close()\n121\t\t}\n122\t}\n123\t\n124\t// Archive runs the archive job to move old events to the archive table.\n125\tfunc (e *EventsHandler) Archive(_ interface{}) {\n126\t\tevents.RunArchiveJob(e.db)\n127\t}\n128\t\n129\t// createEventsSchema creates the events, events_archive, and FTS5 tables.\n130\tfunc createEventsSchema(db *sql.DB) error {\n131\t\tschema := `\n132\t\tCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS events (\n133\t\t\tid          INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n134\t\t\ttimestamp_ms INTEGER NOT NULL,\n135\t\t\ttype        TEXT    NOT NULL,\n136\t\t\tzone        TEXT,\n137\t\t\tperson      TEXT,\n138\t\t\tblob_id     INTEGER,\n139\t\t\tdetail_json TEXT,\n140\t\t\tseverity    TEXT    NOT NULL DEFAULT 'info'\n141\t\t);\n142\t\tCREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_events_time ON events(timestamp_ms DESC);\n143\t\tCREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_events_type ON events(type, timestamp_ms DESC);\n144\t\tCREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_events_zone ON events(zone, timestamp_ms DESC);\n145\t\tCREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_events_person ON events(person, timestamp_ms DESC);\n146\t\tCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS events_archive (\n147\t\t\tid          INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,\n148\t\t\ttimestamp_ms INTEGER NOT NULL,\n149\t\t\ttype        TEXT    NOT NULL,\n150\t\t\tzone        TEXT,\n151\t\t\tperson      TEXT,\n152\t\t\tblob_id     INTEGER,\n153\t\t\tdetail_json TEXT,\n154\t\t\tseverity    TEXT    NOT NULL DEFAULT 'info'\n155\t\t);\n156\t\tCREATE VIRTUAL TABLE IF NOT EXISTS events_fts USING fts5(\n157\t\t\ttype, zone, person, detail_json,\n158\t\t\tcontent='events', content_rowid='id'\n159\t\t);\n160\t\tCREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS events_fts_insert AFTER INSERT ON events BEGIN\n161\t\t\tINSERT INTO events_fts(rowid, type, zone, person, detail_json)\n162\t\t\tVALUES (new.id, new.type, new.zone, new.person, new.detail_json);\n163\t\tEND;\n164\t\tCREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS events_fts_delete AFTER DELETE ON events BEGIN\n165\t\t\tINSERT INTO events_fts(events_fts, rowid, type, zone, person, detail_json)\n166\t\t\tVALUES ('delete', old.id, old.type, old.zone, old.person, old.detail_json);\n167\t\tEND;\n168\t\tCREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS events_fts_update AFTER UPDATE ON events BEGIN\n169\t\t\tINSERT INTO events_fts(events_fts, rowid, type, zone, person, detail_json)\n170\t\t\tVALUES ('delete', old.id, old.type, old.zone, old.person, old.detail_json);\n171\t\tINSERT INTO events_fts(rowid, type, zone, person, detail_json)\n172\t\tVALUES (new.id, new.type, new.zone, new.person, new.detail_json);\n173\t\tEND;\n174\t\t`\n175\t\t_, err := db.Exec(schema)\n176\t\treturn err\n177\t}\n178\t\n179\t// isValidEventType checks whether the event type string is a known type.\n180\tfunc isValidEventType(t string) bool {\n181\t\tswitch t {\n182\t\tcase \"detection\", \"zone_entry\", \"zone_exit\", \"portal_crossing\",\n183\t\t\t\"trigger_fired\", \"fall_alert\", \"FallDetected\", \"anomaly\", \"AnomalyDetected\", \"security_alert\",\n184\t\t\t\"node_online\", \"node_offline\", \"ota_update\", \"baseline_changed\",\n185\t\t\t\"system\", \"learning_milestone\", \"sleep_session_end\", \"ZoneTransition\",\n186\t\t\t\"presence_transition\", \"stationary_detected\", \"anomaly_learned\", \"sleep_session_start\":\n187\t\t\treturn true\n188\t\t}\n189\t\treturn false\n190\t}\n191\t\n192\t// RegisterRoutes registers events endpoints.\n193\t//\n194\t// GET /api/events — paginated event list with FTS5 search and keyset cursor pagination.\n195\t//\n196\t//\tQuery params: limit (default 50, max 500), before (timestamp_ms cursor),\n197\t//\tsince (ISO8601), until (ISO8601), type (single type filter),\n198\t//\ttypes (comma-separated type list for category filtering),\n199\t//\tzone, zone_id, person, person_id, q (FTS5 query), mode (expert|simple).\n200\t//\n201\t// GET /api/events/{id} — single event by ID.\n202\t//\n203\t// POST /api/events/{id}/feedback — submit feedback for an event.\n204\tfunc (e *EventsHandler) RegisterRoutes(r chi.Router) {\n205\t\tr.Get(\"/api/events\", e.listEvents)\n206\t\tr.Get(\"/api/events/{id}\", e.getEvent)\n207\t\tr.Post(\"/api/events/{id}/feedback\", e.postEventFeedback)\n208\t}\n209\t\n210\t// eventsResponse is the JSON response for GET /api/events.\n211\ttype eventsResponse struct {\n212\t\tEvents        []*Event `json:\"events\"`\n213\t\tCursor        string   `json:\"cursor,omitempty\"`\n214\t\tHasMore       bool     `json:\"has_more\"`\n215\t\tTotalFiltered int      `json:\"total_filtered\"`\n216\t}\n217\t\n218\t// prepareFTSQuery appends a trailing * for prefix matching if the query\n219\t// doesn't already end with a FTS5 operator character. This enables\n220\t// partial word matching (e.g., \"kit\" matches \"kitchen\").\n221\tfunc prepareFTSQuery(q string) string {\n222\t\tq = strings.TrimSpace(q)\n223\t\tif q == \"\" {\n224\t\t\treturn q\n225\t\t}\n226\t\t// If the query already ends with a FTS5 special character or operator, leave it alone.\n227\t\tlast := q[len(q)-1]\n228\t\tif last == '*' || last == '\"' || last == ')' {\n229\t\t\treturn q\n230\t\t}\n231\t\t// For simple terms (no operators), append * for prefix matching.\n232\t\t// If the query contains FTS5 operators (AND, OR, NOT, NEAR), append * to each\n233\t\t// simple token instead.\n234\t\tif strings.Contains(q, \" AND \") || strings.Contains(q, \" OR \") ||\n235\t\t\tstrings.Contains(q, \" NOT \") || strings.Contains(q, \" NEAR \") {\n236\t\t\t// Has operators — append * to each token that isn't an operator or quoted phrase.\n237\t\t\tparts := strings.Fields(q)\n238\t\t\tfor i, p := range parts {\n239\t\t\t\tif p == \"AND\" || p == \"OR\" || p == \"NOT\" || p == \"NEAR\" {\n240\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n241\t\t\t\t}\n242\t\t\t\tif (strings.HasPrefix(p, `\"`) && strings.HasSuffix(p, `\"`)) || p == \"(\" || p == \")\" {\n243\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n244\t\t\t\t}\n245\t\t\t\tparts[i] = p + \"*\"\n246\t\t\t}\n247\t\t\treturn strings.Join(parts, \" \")\n248\t\t}\n249\t\t// Simple single-term query — just append * for prefix matching.\n250\t\treturn q + \"*\"\n251\t}\n252\t\n253\tfunc (e *EventsHandler) listEvents(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n254\t\t// Parse limit\n255\t\tlimit := eventsDefaultLimit\n256\t\tif s := r.URL.Query().Get(\"limit\"); s != \"\" {\n257\t\t\tif n, err := strconv.Atoi(s); err == nil && n > 0 {\n258\t\t\t\tlimit = n\n259\t\t\t}\n260\t\t}\n261\t\tif limit > eventsMaxLimit {\n262\t\t\tlimit = eventsMaxLimit\n263\t\t}\n264\t\n265\t\t// Parse before cursor (timestamp_ms as string)\n266\t\tvar beforeTS int64\n267\t\tif s := r.URL.Query().Get(\"before\"); s != \"\" {\n268\t\t\tbeforeTS, _ = strconv.ParseInt(s, 10, 64)\n269\t\t}\n270\t\n271\t\t// Parse filters\n272\t\tq := r.URL.Query().Get(\"q\")\n273\t\teventType := r.URL.Query().Get(\"type\")\n274\t\ttypesStr := r.URL.Query().Get(\"types\") // comma-separated list of event types\n275\t\tzone := r.URL.Query().Get(\"zone\")\n276\t\tzoneID := r.URL.Query().Get(\"zone_id\")\n277\t\tif zoneID != \"\" {\n278\t\t\tzone = zoneID // zone_id takes precedence over zone\n279\t\t}\n280\t\tperson := r.URL.Query().Get(\"person\")\n281\t\tpersonID := r.URL.Query().Get(\"person_id\")\n282\t\tif personID != \"\" {\n283\t\t\tperson = personID // person_id takes precedence over person\n284\t\t}\n285\t\tafterStr := r.URL.Query().Get(\"after\")\n286\t\tsinceStr := r.URL.Query().Get(\"since\") // Alias for after\n287\t\tuntilStr := r.URL.Query().Get(\"until\") // Upper bound timestamp\n288\t\tmode := r.URL.Query().Get(\"mode\")      // \"expert\" or \"simple\" (default: simple)\n289\t\n290\t\t// Parse and validate types list (comma-separated)\n291\t\tvar typesFilter []string\n292\t\tif typesStr != \"\" {\n293\t\t\tfor _, t := range strings.Split(typesStr, \",\") {\n294\t\t\t\tt = strings.TrimSpace(t)\n295\t\t\t\tif t == \"\" {\n296\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n297\t\t\t\t}\n298\t\t\t\tif !isValidEventType(t) {\n299\t\t\t\t\twriteJSONError(w, http.StatusBadRequest, \"invalid event type: \"+t)\n300\t\t\t\t\treturn\n301\t\t\t\t}\n302\t\t\t\ttypesFilter = append(typesFilter, t)\n303\t\t\t}\n304\t\t}\n305\t\n306\t\t// Validate event type\n307\t\tif eventType != \"\" && !isValidEventType(eventType) {\n308\t\t\twriteJSONError(w, http.StatusBadRequest, \"invalid event type\")\n309\t\t\treturn\n310\t\t}\n311\t\n312\t\t// Validate after/since timestamp (prefer since if both provided)\n313\t\tvar afterTS int64\n314\t\ttimeStr := afterStr\n315\t\tif sinceStr != \"\" {\n316\t\t\ttimeStr = sinceStr\n317\t\t}\n318\t\tif timeStr != \"\" {\n319\t\t\tt, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339, timeStr)\n320\t\t\tif err != nil {\n321\t\t\t\twriteJSONError(w, http.StatusBadRequest, \"invalid since/after timestamp\")\n322\t\t\t\treturn\n323\t\t\t}\n324\t\t\tafterTS = t.UnixNano() / 1e6\n325\t\t}\n326\t\n327\t\t// Validate until timestamp (upper bound)\n328\t\tvar untilTS int64\n329\t\tif untilStr != \"\" {\n330\t\t\tt, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339, untilStr)\n331\t\t\tif err != nil {\n332\t\t\t\twriteJSONError(w, http.StatusBadRequest, \"invalid until timestamp\")\n333\t\t\t\treturn\n334\t\t\t}\n335\t\t\tuntilTS = t.UnixNano() / 1e6\n336\t\t}\n337\t\n338\t\t// Person-relevant event types for simple mode\n339\t\t// Simple mode shows only person-relevant events: zone_entry, zone_exit, ZoneTransition, portal_crossing, fall_alert, FallDetected, anomaly, AnomalyDetected, security_alert, sleep_session_end\n340\t\t// Simple mode hides: node_online, node_offline, ota_update, baseline_changed, system, learning_milestone, detection, presence_transition, stationary_detected\n341\t\tsimpleModeTypes := map[string]bool{\n342\t\t\t\"zone_entry\":        true,\n343\t\t\t\"zone_exit\":         true,\n344\t\t\t\"ZoneTransition\":    true,\n345\t\t\t\"portal_crossing\":   true,\n346\t\t\t\"fall_alert\":        true,\n347\t\t\t\"FallDetected\":      true,\n348\t\t\t\"anomaly\":           true,\n349\t\t\t\"AnomalyDetected\":   true,\n350\t\t\t\"security_alert\":    true,\n351\t\t\t\"sleep_session_end\": true,\n352\t\t}\n353\t\t// Default to expert mode; switch to simple mode only when explicitly requested\n354\t\tisSimpleMode := mode == \"simple\"\n355\t\n356\t\t// Prepare FTS5 query with prefix matching\n357\t\tif q != \"\" {\n358\t\t\tq = prepareFTSQuery(q)\n359\t\t}\n360\t\n361\t\t// Determine query mode: FTS5 or regular\n362\t\tuseFTS := q != \"\"\n363\t\tp := \"\" // column prefix for FTS JOIN queries\n364\t\tif useFTS {\n365\t\t\tp = \"e.\"\n366\t\t}\n367\t\n368\t\t// Build SELECT columns and FROM clause\n369\t\tselectCols := p + \"id, \" + p + \"timestamp_ms, \" + p + \"type, \" + p + \"zone, \" +\n370\t\t\tp + \"person, \" + p + \"blob_id, \" + p + \"detail_json, \" + p + \"severity\"\n371\t\n372\t\tvar fromTable, baseWhere string\n373\t\tvar baseArgs []interface{}\n374\t\n375\t\tif useFTS {\n376\t\t\tfromTable = \"events e JOIN events_fts ft ON e.id = ft.rowid\"\n377\t\t\tbaseWhere = \"events_fts MATCH ?\"\n378\t\t\tbaseArgs = []interface{}{q}\n379\t\t} else {\n380\t\t\tfromTable = \"events\"\n381\t\t\tbaseWhere = \"1=1\"\n382\t\t\tbaseArgs = []interface{}{}\n383\t\t}\n384\t\n385\t\t// Build WHERE clause with filters\n386\t\twhereSQL := baseWhere\n387\t\twhereArgs := append([]interface{}{}, baseArgs...)\n388\t\n389\t\tif eventType != \"\" {\n390\t\t\twhereSQL += \" AND \" + p + \"type = ?\"\n391\t\t\twhereArgs = append(whereArgs, eventType)\n392\t\t} else if len(typesFilter) > 0 {\n393\t\t\t// Multiple type filter (from category checkboxes)\n394\t\t\tph := make([]string, len(typesFilter))\n395\t\t\tfor i := range ph {\n396\t\t\t\tph[i] = \"?\"\n397\t\t\t}\n398\t\t\twhereSQL += \" AND \" + p + \"type IN (\" + strings.Join(ph, \", \") + \")\"\n399\t\t\tfor _, t := range typesFilter {\n400\t\t\t\twhereArgs = append(whereArgs, t)\n401\t\t\t}\n402\t\t} else if isSimpleMode {\n403\t\t\t// In simple mode with no explicit type filter, only show person-relevant event types\n404\t\t\t// Build IN clause for simple mode types\n405\t\t\tsimpleTypeList := make([]string, 0, len(simpleModeTypes))\n406\t\t\tfor eventType := range simpleModeTypes {\n407\t\t\t\tsimpleTypeList = append(simpleTypeList, eventType)\n408\t\t\t}\n409\t\t\t// Build placeholder string for IN clause\n410\t\t\tplaceholders := make([]string, len(simpleTypeList))\n411\t\t\tfor i := range placeholders {\n412\t\t\t\tplaceholders[i] = \"?\"\n413\t\t\t}\n414\t\t\twhereSQL += \" AND \" + p + \"type IN (\" + strings.Join(placeholders, \", \") + \")\"\n415\t\t\tfor _, eventType := range simpleTypeList {\n416\t\t\t\twhereArgs = append(whereArgs, eventType)\n417\t\t\t}\n418\t\t}\n419\t\tif zone != \"\" {\n420\t\t\twhereSQL += \" AND \" + p + \"zone = ?\"\n421\t\t\twhereArgs = append(whereArgs, zone)\n422\t\t}\n423\t\tif person != \"\" {\n424\t\t\twhereSQL += \" AND \" + p + \"person = ?\"\n425\t\t\twhereArgs = append(whereArgs, person)\n426\t\t}\n427\t\tif afterTS > 0 {\n428\t\t\twhereSQL += \" AND \" + p + \"timestamp_ms >= ?\"\n429\t\t\twhereArgs = append(whereArgs, afterTS)\n430\t\t}\n431\t\tif untilTS > 0 {\n432\t\t\t// Use < untilTS+1000 to include the entire second when the until timestamp\n433\t\t\t// is in second precision (RFC3339 format truncates sub-seconds).\n434\t\t\twhereSQL += \" AND \" + p + \"timestamp_ms < ?\"\n435\t\t\twhereArgs = append(whereArgs, untilTS+1000)\n436\t\t}\n437\t\n438\t\t// COUNT for total_filtered\n439\t\tcountSQL := \"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM \" + fromTable + \" WHERE \" + whereSQL\n440\t\tvar totalFiltered int\n441\t\tif err := e.db.QueryRow(countSQL, whereArgs...).Scan(&totalFiltered); err != nil {\n442\t\t\twriteJSONError(w, http.StatusInternalServerError, \"failed to count events\")\n443\t\t\treturn\n444\t\t}\n445\t\n446\t\t// Data query: add before cursor + ordering + limit\n447\t\tdataWhere := whereSQL\n448\t\tdataArgs := append([]interface{}{}, whereArgs...)\n449\t\tif beforeTS > 0 {\n450\t\t\tdataWhere += \" AND \" + p + \"timestamp_ms < ?\"\n451\t\t\tdataArgs = append(dataArgs, beforeTS)\n452\t\t}\n453\t\t// untilTS is already included in the base WHERE clause via whereArgs\n454\t\n455\t\tdataSQL := \"SELECT \" + selectCols + \" FROM \" + fromTable +\n456\t\t\t\" WHERE \" + dataWhere +\n457\t\t\t\" ORDER BY \" + p + \"timestamp_ms DESC, \" + p + \"id DESC\" +\n458\t\t\t\" LIMIT ?\"\n459\t\tdataArgs = append(dataArgs, limit+1)\n460\t\n461\t\trows, err := e.db.Query(dataSQL, dataArgs...)\n462\t\tif err != nil {\n463\t\t\twriteJSONError(w, http.StatusInternalServerError, \"failed to query events\")\n464\t\t\treturn\n465\t\t}\n466\t\tdefer rows.Close()\n467\t\n468\t\tevents := make([]*Event, 0, limit)\n469\t\tfor rows.Next() {\n470\t\t\tvar ev Event\n471\t\t\tif err := rows.Scan(&ev.ID, &ev.Timestamp, &ev.Type, &ev.Zone,\n472\t\t\t\t&ev.Person, &ev.BlobID, &ev.DetailJSON, &ev.Severity); err != nil {\n473\t\t\t\tcontinue\n474\t\t\t}\n475\t\t\tevents = append(events, &ev)\n476\t\t}\n477\t\n478\t\thasMore := len(events) > limit\n479\t\tif hasMore {\n480\t\t\tevents = events[:limit]\n481\t\t}\n482\t\n483\t\tcursor := \"\"\n484\t\tif hasMore && len(events) > 0 {\n485\t\t\tcursor = strconv.FormatInt(events[len(events)-1].Timestamp, 10)\n486\t\t}\n487\t\n488\t\twriteJSON(w, http.StatusOK, eventsResponse{\n489\t\t\tEvents:        events,\n490\t\t\tCursor:        cursor,\n491\t\t\tHasMore:       hasMore,\n492\t\t\tTotalFiltered: totalFiltered,\n493\t\t})\n494\t}\n495\t\n496\tfunc (e *EventsHandler) getEvent(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n497\t\tidStr := chi.URLParam(r, \"id\")\n498\t\tid, err := strconv.ParseInt(idStr, 10, 64)\n499\t\tif err != nil {\n500\t\t\twriteJSONError(w, http.StatusBadRequest, \"invalid event id\")\n501\t\t\treturn\n502\t\t}\n503\t\n504\t\tvar event Event\n505\t\terr = e.db.QueryRow(`\n506\t\t\tSELECT id, timestamp_ms, type, zone, person, blob_id, detail_json, severity\n507\t\t\tFROM events\n508\t\t\tWHERE id = ?\n509\t\t`, id).Scan(&event.ID, &event.Timestamp, &event.Type, &event.Zone,\n510\t\t\t&event.Person, &event.BlobID, &event.DetailJSON, &event.Severity)\n511\t\tif err == sql.ErrNoRows {\n512\t\t\twriteJSONError(w, http.StatusNotFound, \"event not found\")\n513\t\t\treturn\n514\t\t} else if err != nil {\n515\t\t\twriteJSONError(w, http.StatusInternalServerError, \"failed to query event\")\n516\t\t\treturn\n517\t\t}\n518\t\n519\t\twriteJSON(w, http.StatusOK, event)\n520\t}\n521\t\n522\t// postEventFeedback handles POST /api/events/{id}/feedback\n523\t// It delegates to the feedback module after validating the event exists.\n524\tfunc (e *EventsHandler) postEventFeedback(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n525\t\tidStr := chi.URLParam(r, \"id\")\n526\t\teventID, err := strconv.ParseInt(idStr, 10, 64)\n527\t\tif err != nil err != nil {\n62\t\t\tlockFile.Close()\n63\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"acquire flock on %s (another instance running?): %w\", lockPath, err)\n64\t\t}\n65\t\tdone()\n66\t\n67\t\t// Phase 2: SQLite open\n68\t\tstartup.CheckTimeout(ctx)\n69\t\tdone = startup.Phase(2, \"SQLite\")\n70\t\tdb, err := sql.Open(\"sqlite\", dbPath+\"?_pragma=journal_mode(WAL)&_pragma=synchronous(NORMAL)&_pragma=foreign_keys(ON)&_pragma=busy_timeout(5000)\")\n71\t\tif err != nil {\n72\t\t\tlockFile.Close()\n73\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open sqlite: %w\", err)\n74\t\t}\n75\t\tdb.SetMaxOpenConns(1) // SQLite is single-writer\n76\t\n77\t\tif err := db.PingContext(ctx); renameErr != nil {\n91\t\t\t\tlockFile.Close()\n92\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"move corrupt database: %w\", renameErr)\n93\t\t\t}\n94\t\t\tdb, err = sql.Open(\"sqlite\", dbPath+\"?_pragma=journal_mode(WAL)&_pragma=synchronous(NORMAL)&_pragma=foreign_keys(ON)&_pragma=busy_timeout(5000)\")\n95\t\t\tif err != nil {\n96\t\t\t\tlockFile.Close()\n97\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open fresh sqlite: %w\", err)\n98\t\t\t}\n99\t\t\tdb.SetMaxOpenConns(1)\n100\t\t}\n101\t\tdone()\n102\t\n103\t\t// Phase 3: Schema migration\n104\t\tstartup.CheckTimeout(ctx)\n105\t\tdone = startup.Phase(3, \"Schema migrations\")\n106\t\tmigrator, err := NewMigrator(dbPath, Config{\n107\t\t\tDataDir:         dataDir,\n108\t\t\tBackupRetention: 90 * 24 * time.Hour,\n109\t\t})\n110\t\tif err != nil {\n111\t\t\tdb.Close()\n112\t\t\tlockFile.Close()\n113\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"create migrator: %w\", err)\n114\t\t}\n115\t\tmigrator.Register(AllMigrations()...)\n116\t\n117\t\tcurrent, err := migrator.CurrentVersion(ctx)\n118\t\tif err != nil {\n119\t\t\tdb.Close()\n120\t\t\tlockFile.Close()\n121\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"get current version: %w\", err)\n122\t\t}\n123\t\n124\t\tif current == 0 {\n125\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] Initializing new database\")\n126\t\t} else {\n127\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] Current schema version %d\", current)\n128\t\t}\n129\t\n130\t\tif err := migrator.Migrate(ctx); This enables\n251\t// partial word matching (e.g., \"kit\" matches \"kitchen\").\n252\tfunc prepareFTSQuery(q string) string {\n253\t\tq = strings.TrimSpace(q)\n254\t\tif q == \"\" {\n255\t\t\treturn q\n256\t\t}\n257\t\t// If the query already ends with a FTS5 special character or operator, leave it alone.\n258\t\tlast := q[len(q)-1]\n259\t\tif last == '*' || last == '\"' || last == ')' time).\n288\tfunc RunArchiveJob(db *sql.DB) error {\n289\t\t// Get the cutoff timestamp\n290\t\tcutoffMs := time.Now().UnixMilli() - ArchiveDaysMs\n291\t\n292\t\t// Begin transaction for atomic ArchiveDays)\n308\t\t\treturn nil\n309\t\t}\n310\t\n311\t\tlog.Printf(\"[events archive] Archiving %d events older than %d days\", count, ArchiveDays)\n312\t\n313\t\t// Copy old events to archive table\n314\t\t// We preserve the original ID to maintain referential integrity\n315\t\t_, err = tx.Exec(`\n316\t\t\tINSERT INTO events_archive (id, timestamp_ms, type, zone, person, blob_id, detail_json, severity)\n317\t\t\tSELECT id, timestamp_ms, type, zone, person, blob_id, detail_json, severity\n318\t\t\tFROM events\n319\t\t\tWHERE timestamp_ms < ?\n320\t\t`, cutoffMs)\n321\t\tif err != nil {\n322\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"copy events to archive: %w\", err)\n323\t\t}\n324\t\n325\t\t// Delete the archived events from the main events table\n326\t\t// The FTS5 triggers will automatically remove them from events_fts\n327\t\tresult, err := tx.Exec(\"DELETE FROM events WHERE timestamp_ms < ?\", cutoffMs)\n328\t\tif err != nil {\n329\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete archived {\n335\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Events archive: copied %d but deleted %d rows\", count, rowsAffected)\n336\t\t}\n337\t\n338\t\tif err := tx.Commit(); err != nil {\n339\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"commit archive transaction: %w\", err)\n340\t\t}\n341\t\n342\t\tlog.Printf(\"[events archive] Successfully archived %d events\", count)\n343\t\treturn nil\n344\t}\n345\t\n346\t// GetEventByID retrieves a single event by its ID.\n347\tfunc GetEventByID(db *sql.DB, id int64) (*Event, error) {\n348\t\tvar e Event\n349\t\terr := db.QueryRow(`\n350\t\t\tSELECT id, timestamp_ms, type, zone, person, blob_id, sql.ErrNoRows {\n355\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"event not found: %d\", id)\n356\t\t}\n357\t\tif err != nil {\n358\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"query event: %w\", err)\n359\t\t}\n360\t\treturn &e, nil\n361\t}\n362\t\n363\t// InsertDetectionEvent is a convenience function for inserting detection events.\n364\tfunc InsertDetectionEvent(db *sql.DB, zone string, person string, blobID int, detail with a FTS5 operator character. This enables\n220\t// partial word matching (e.g., \"kit\" matches \"kitchen\").\n221\tfunc prepareFTSQuery(q string) string {\n222\t\tq = strings.TrimSpace(q)\n223\t\tif q == \"\" {\n224\t\t\treturn q\n225\t\t}\n226\t\t// If the query already ends with a FTS5 special character or operator, leave it alone.\n227\t\tlast := q[len(q)-1]\n228\t\tif last == '*' || last == '\"' || last == ')' {\n229\t\t\treturn q\n230\t\t}\n231\t\t// For simple terms (no operators), append * for prefix matching.\n232\t\t// If the query contains FTS5 operators (AND, OR, NOT, NEAR), append * to each\n233\t\t// simple token instead.\n234\t\tif strings.Contains(q, \" AND \") || strings.Contains(q, \" OR \") ||\n235\t\t\tstrings.Contains(q, \" NOT \") || strings.Contains(q, \" NEAR \") {\n236\t\t\t// Has operators — append * to each token that isn't an operator or quoted phrase.\n237\t\t\tparts := strings.Fields(q)\n238\t\t\tfor i, p := range parts {\n239\t\t\t\tif p == \"AND\" || p == \"OR\" || p == \"NOT\" || p == \"NEAR\" {\n240\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n241\t\t\t\t}\n242\t\t\t\tif (strings.HasPrefix(p, `\"`) && strings.HasSuffix(p, `\"`)) || p == \"(\" || p == \")\" {\n243\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n244\t\t\t\t}\n245\t\t\t\tparts[i] = p + \"*\"\n246\t\t\t}\n247\t\t\treturn strings.Join(parts, \" \")\n248\t\t}\n249\t\t// Simple single-term query — just append * for prefix matching.\n250\t\treturn q + \"*\"\n251\t}\n252\t\n253\tfunc (e *EventsHandler) listEvents(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n254\t\t// Parse limit\n255\t\tlimit := labels.\n338\tfunc (h *ZonesHandler) resolvePeople(blobIDs []int) []string {\n339\t\th.mu.RLock()\n340\t\tident := h.ident\n341\t\th.mu.RUnlock()\n342\t\n343\t\tif ident == nil || len(blobIDs) == 0 people\n357\t}\n358\t\n359\t// toPortalResponse converts a zones.Portal to the API response format.\n360\tfunc toPortalResponse(p *zones.Portal) portalWithZones {\n361\t\treturn zones with current occupancy.\n388\tfunc (h *ZonesHandler) listZones(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n389\t\tallZones := h.mgr.GetAllZones()\n390\t\th.mu.RLock()\n391\t\tdefer Auto-generates an ID if none is provided.\n402\tfunc (h *ZonesHandler) createZone(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n403\t\tvar zone zones.Zone\n404\t\tif err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&zone); type.\n345\t// The send is non-blocking; if a subscriber's channel is full, the event is skipped.\n346\t// This prevents a slow subscriber from blocking the entire system.\n347\t// Returns the number
